# Leisure Centre Knowledge Base

## Albany Creek

### Contact Information
Albany Creek Contact Information: Albany Creek Leisure Centre contact details: Phone 07 3264 9900, Email albanycreek@belgravialeisure.com.au, Website https://albanycreeklc.com.au, Facebook page Albany Creek Leisure Centre & Health Club located in Albany Creek QLD.

### Opening Hours
Albany Creek Opening Hours: Albany Creek Leisure Centre Operating Hours Year Round: Monday to Thursday 5am to 8pm, Friday 5am to 8pm, Saturday 6am to 6pm, Sunday 7am to 5pm. Pools will close 15 minutes prior to centre closing hours. Public Holidays 10am to 4pm times may vary. Health Club has 24 hour access available. Playroom Hours Monday to Friday 9am to 12.15pm, Saturday 7am to 12pm.

### Membership Prices and Options
Albany Creek Membership: Albany Creek Health Club fully refurbished November 2024 with all new gym equipment. Direct Debit and Upfront Options available. Physio Insurance memberships available in one or three month duration refer customer to site for processing. 2025-2026 Membership Prices: Full Access Membership Adult $26.95 per week Concession $22.95 per week $45 joining fee includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes land and water Health Club Access Begin optional 24 Hour Tag $39.95 once off optional Creche membership $5 weekly. Swimming Membership Adult $20.50 per week Concession $16.50 per week $20 joining fee includes Swimming Pools Access. Full Access FIFO ONLY $13.50 per week $45 joining fee includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes Health Club Access optional 24 Hour Tag $39.95 once off optional Creche $5 weekly. Premium Membership $52.95 per week $45 joining fee includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes Health Club Access Free Creche Membership Free 24 Hour Tag B-Active Functional Training BAFT Reformer Pilates existing 2024-2025 Premium members remain $49.95. DVA Full Access 12 month Membership $690 includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes Health Club Access optional 24 Hour Tag $39.95 once off optional Creche $5 weekly refer to venue before purchasing. Aquatic Access 12 Months Adult $665.50 Concession $538.45 includes Swimming Pool Access. Full Access 1 month Traveller $125 includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes Health Club Access optional 24 Hour Tag $39.95. Full Access 12 Months Adult $1235 Concession $1110 includes Swimming Pools Access Group Fitness Classes Health Club Access optional 24 Hour Tag $39.95 optional Creche $5 weekly. Childcare Membership $5 per week $10 joining fee for children aged up to 12 years only for Full Access Coaching Zone or Wellness membership joining fee does not apply if family member already a member. Direct Debit options for PT available refer customer to venue. If family member already a member joining fee does not apply as one joining fee per family charged.

### Fitness Passport
Albany Creek Fitness Passport: Albany Creek Fitness Passport members are not entitled to 24 hour access. They are not able to utilise the $5 weekly creche membership and will have to pay casually if booking in for creche. Fitness Passport members are entitled to a 30 minute induction with a trainer to show them around. However they do not get access to the BEGIN program offered to members. If they join the $36 premium Fitness Passport membership they are entitled to everything above with benefits being free creche free 24 hour tag and option to utilise BEGIN. Wellness Membership and Coaching Zone are not included for Fitness Passport. Fitness Passport members can purchase a reduced rate of $36 per week on top of their Fitness Passport Membership if they wish to avail Wellness Reformer and Coaching Zone membership.

### Concessions and Discounts
Albany Creek Concessions and Discounts: Albany Creek eligible concession cards include Health Care Card, Student Card, Seniors Card, Carer Card. Holders of a companion card can attend the gym with members free of charge and can observe monitor support classes free of charge. Companion card holders only pay concession rate if they are actively taking part in the class. Mount Barker Swim Club Members do not get charged a joining fee and need to join as members onsite to receive this discount. To process in AW apply the discount and use the Promo Code SWIMCLUB.

### Casual Entry and Visit Passes
Albany Creek Casual rates: Albany Creek Casual Swim Fees 2025/2026: Adult 16 years and over $6.65 casual entry or $179.70 for 30 visit pass, Child Entry $5.80 casual or $156.60 for 30 visit pass, Seniors Entry Aged and Disability $5.30 casual or $143.20 for 30 visit pass, Children Under 3 Years Free, Water Slide Pass $7.00 in addition to general entry fee, Family Pool Entry max 4 people including 1 Adult $21.05, Extra Family Member with Family Pool Entry $5.25, Non Swimmer Fee not including programs spectators $4.00. 30 visit passes have 6 month expiry. Casual Aqua Class 2025/2026: Adult Aqua Class $21.60 casual entry or $194.40 for 10 visit pass, Seniors Aqua Class $16.70 casual entry or $150.65 for 10 visit pass.

### Group Fitness
Albany Creek Group Fitness: Albany Creek Leisure Centre class timetables and schedules: Group Fitness timetable available at https://www.albanycreeklc.com.au/getmedia/0abfe77b-1d9b-40d5-a09b-52a4a53bb8ae/group-exercise-timetable-summer-2024.pdf, Aqua Classes timetable available at https://www.albanycreeklc.com.au/getmedia/78cc9b53-c14b-49ca-8c85-2117a28f4a22/Aqua-Timetable-CD.pdf, Reformer Pilates timetable available at https://www.albanycreeklc.com.au/getmedia/16a88d21-beaf-4aa5-80aa-a1c33f98f42a/Reformer-Pilates-Timetable.pdf. For current class schedules times and availability please refer to these timetables or contact the centre.

### Reformer Pilates
Albany Creek Reformer Pilates: Albany Creek Leisure Centre and Health Club Reformer Pilates studio. Casual Reformer Pilates class $35. Using spring loaded resistance on a reformer bed instructors guide you through exercises designed to increase strength mobility coordination and balance. Studio has 10 reformer beds with wide selection of classes per week. Reformer pilates suited to all fitness levels and skills. Book via Active World membership app up to 3 days in advance. Premium Membership includes unlimited access to reformer pilates classes plus full access to gym B-Active Functional Training group fitness classes pools and playroom for $49.95 per week.

### Childcare
Albany Creek Childcare: Albany Creek Leisure Centre Playroom provides members with informal adjunct care for children. Maximum 1 hour in care per child per day please book to avoid disappointment. All staff first aid trained and have blue cards. Playroom open for children 8 weeks old to 6 years of age. School children under 12 years accepted during school holidays. Cancellation of booking must be done via Active World app or contact center before 7am on the day. Nut Free Zone including almond meal almond milk hummus Nutella banana bread with nuts and mortadella containing pistachios. Session Times Monday to Friday 8am to 9am 9am to 10am 10am to 11am 11am to 12pm. Saturday 7am to 8am 8am to 9am 9am to 10am 10am to 11am. Limited numbers per time slot. To book childcare parent must complete Playroom Enrolment Booklet and attach to child member profile. Active World does not allow booking without this document attached.

### Aquatic Programs
Albany Creek Aquatic Programs: Albany Creek Splish Splash Aqua Playgroup for babies 3 to 6 months old. Designed for parents guardians and adults to participate with baby in water. Great for first time water experience. Babies can start from 3 months to splash and play getting familiar and comfortable in the water helping baby become familiar and explore. Use bath time at home to get baby used to being washed in water. After Splish Splash babies can progress into Learn to Swim program joining Starfish Level catering to infants 6 to 12 months to develop water confidence and swimming safety. Sessions twice a week with casual pay per session option. Download Active World app and pay online arrive 10 minutes early enjoy 30 minute session. Benefits include joint activity for parent and baby paced to suit different levels of ability low impact nutritious exercise. Parents and Babies Aquatic Fitness PABA Fit program also available for parents with babies 6 to 36 months. PABA Fit focuses on parent fitness and bonding paced to suit different ability levels. Low impact high energy fat burning aquatic workout with exercises designed with baby age and development in mind. Classes every Tuesday 11:15am and Friday 11:30am. Class cost $10 per session. Download Active World app and pay online.

### General Information
Albany Creek General Information: Albany Creek Leisure Centre water slides only available on weekends and on public holidays. Albany Creek memberships powered by Active World app technology. App designed to improve communication and interaction between members and team. Become a member by joining or downloading app and using code ALBANY_CREEK. Self managed personal portal features: manage personal and billing details, manage account details, update payment details, check next payment date, buy new membership or visit pass, scan in using digital access card when you forget your pass, book into Group Fitness Classes, view upcoming classes, send and receive messages to Centre staff.

Accredited exercise physiologists (AEPs) are university qualified, allied health professionals with the knowledge, skills and competencies to serve those with acute, sub-acute or chronic medical conditions, injuries or disabilities. If you have Private Health insurance or you're currently under WorkCover, TAC, DVA or NDIS funding streams you may qualify for rebates under these compensable schemes. Pathology domains covered by the services of AEPs include: Kidney• Cancers• Metabolic• Neurological• Cardiovascular• Musculoskeletal• Respiratory/pulmonary and mental health• Any other conditions for which there is evidence that exercise can improve the client’s clinical status. • 1:1 Session Fees Group Exercise Physiology The following steps apply for people to access it: Exercise Physiology Tuesday, June 17, 2025 12:26 PM Step 1 - Upgrade or Join This must be done with staff over the phone or in person, and is not available on the website. The membership is listed under the heading 'Exercise Physiology, MOVE Gold 2.0'. *Existing Gold members can access this but need to have their membership changed to MOVE Gold 2.0 Step 2 - Book into a consult with an EP This needs to be done prior to attending any group sessions as they will need to have their program written up by the EP. This can be done here: https://book.nookal.com/bookings/book/e0a7fAcB-8C36-c27C-a238-65E33E491eac/location/PZSBR Click 'any available practitioner' or Claudia, and then select MOVE Gold Membership, Initial Assessment Step 3 - Book into group sessions! Sessions can be booked via ActiveWorld, the same way that you would book a group fitness class but search exercise physiology instead. Group EP gym sessions will run at the following times: Monday 12pm-1pm AVLC Wednesday 4.30pm-5.30pm KELC Thursday 4pm-5pm AVLC 4 personal trainers available Cat (external PT, sets her own prices)• Trish• Drey (head coach, functional training)• Stefan• 10 x visit PT passes available for 30 or 60 minute sessions Personal Training Tuesday, June 17, 2025 12:22 PM Childcare Fees 2025/26 Standard Concession MOVE Member Casual Creche $7.65 $5.45 MOVE Member Occasional Care $8.85 $6.40 MOVE Member 10x Creche Sessions $63.90 $45.65 MOVE Member 25x Creche Sessions $149.65 $107.75 Casual Creche Fee $14.10 $9.95 Occasional Care $18.40 $13.25 10x Casual Creche Sessions $126.60 $90.85 25x Casual Creche Sessions $299.25 $215.45 For children aged 6 weeks to 8 years old.• Childcare Opening Hours Our operating hours are Monday to Friday (excluding public holidays). Please Note Bookings are essential.• You are required to provide your child's immunisation history.• Before your child can be left in the care of our childcare staff, a fully completed enrolment form along with a copy of your child’s immunisation details must be submitted. • Parents will be required to attend an in-person induction session prior to commencing childcare sessions. • Availability and Childcare Bookings Childcare and occasional care are available to both members and non-members. Sessions can be booked back-to-back and can be made on a casual basis or up to two weeks in advance. Casual Childcare - these are sessions available to parents and guardians that are staying in the centre and utilising the facilities (e.g., to have a swim, do a workout or attend a group fitness class). Occasional Care - these are sessions for parents and guardians that need to leave the centre (e.g., to attend work, an appointment, run errands etc) Childcare Tuesday, June 17, 2025 12:21 PM Accessibility Tuesday, June 17, 2025 12:23 PM Pool Temperatures: 25m Pool –29 degrees Warm Water Pool –33-34 degrees Learn to Swim Pool –30 degrees Spa –36-37 degrees What is the minimum age to use the gym? ### Opening Hours

### Aquatic Facilities
Bright Aquatic Facilities: Bright Sports Centre offers a 17m indoor swimming pool specifically catering for beginner and intermediate swimmers. This dedicated pool allows tuition to all ages and abilities making learning to swim a great experience. The pool is designed for swimming lessons and aqua classes. Note: At times aqua classes are scheduled, please refer to the group fitness timetable for specific times when there will be limited public space available. Only one lane available for lap swimming during lessons, you'll likely share the lane. Appropriate swimwear must be worn at all times to maintain a clean safe and inviting environment. Clothing other than swimwear can create problems with water clarity pool disinfectant and water filtration systems.

### Group Fitness
Bright Group Fitness: Group Fitness Classes available at Bright Sports Centre. Casual Group Exercise Class prices Regular Class Adult Non Member $13.50 Regular Class Concession Non Member $8.50 Senior Class Non Member $7.50. Aqua aerobics classes available with dedicated timetable. Members can book into group fitness classes via Active World app. Contact centre at 03 8727 8930 for specific class schedules and timetable details.

### Gym and Fitness Facilities
Bright Gym and Fitness Facilities: Bright Sports Centre features a brand new fully equipped gymnasium operating seven days a week. Cardio equipment includes 3 treadmills 2 cross trainers 5 stationary bikes 3 rowers assault bike ski erg Matrix climbmill. Strength training equipment includes 2 squat racks smith machine dumbbells up to 40kg kettlebells up to 24kg and a wide range of Matrix pin loaded machines. Experienced gym instructors available to create personalized workout programs and demonstrate proper equipment use. Out of Hours Key Fobs available for $24 for extended access.

### Aquatic Programs
Bright Aquatic Programs: Bright Sports Centre offers GOswim swimming lessons powered by Swimming Australia for programs from 6 months through to competitive squads. Lesson pricing $20.76 per lesson Direct Debit Only. Private Lessons $62 per child. Adult swimming classes available. Access and Inclusion programs available for swimmers with diverse needs. Casual swimming opportunities available during operating hours. Aqua aerobics classes with dedicated timetable. Contact centre for enrollment and program details.

### Location and Access
Bright Location and Access: Bright Sports Centre is located in the beautiful alpine town of Bright at 47 Gavan Street Bright VIC 3741 less than five minutes from the town centre and hospital. The centre has a 17m indoor heated swimming pool gymnasium and squash courts. Bright has three squash courts with equipment hire available weight machines dumbbells and other workout equipment and bikes and treadmills in the cardio room. The Bright pool and gym is committed to providing accessible facilities to ensure everyone in the community can enjoy the centre. Accessibility features include ramps for easy pool access an accessible change room and designated accessible parking. Companion Card accepted. If you have specific access requirements or need assistance planning your visit please contact the centre at 03 8727 8930. The team is happy to help ensure you have a comfortable and enjoyable experience.

### General Information
Bright General Information: Bright Sports Centre offers kiosk and shop facilities on site. Pool party bookings available for events. Allied health professional support available at the centre. Active World membership app provides member management allowing users to manage personal and billing details book into group fitness classes view upcoming classes and utilize digital access card. Members can contact centre staff via the membership enquiry option for personalized recommendations. Squash courts available but equipment not available for hire bring your own equipment. The Bundaberg Regional Aquatic Facility will be co-located with the Bundaberg Multiplex, which includes a large modern conference centre and the Bundaberg PCYC. This will leverage previous investments and create a defined, branded high performance-based precinct. A new, FINA standard, covered, 50m, heated competition pool will support regional and state level events and training camps. Additional indoor heated pools and multi-purpose rooms will be available for fitness, teaching and therapy programs, creating a facility able to offer a range of comprehensive health and fitness services. ### Membership Prices and Options
Danny Frawley Membership: 30 days cancellation policy, $5 suspension Policy across all membership. Max 2 reformer pilates classes per week on Platinum & Gold Memberships as it is not considered a Wellness class. Prices for Upfront Silver and Gold Memberships 3 month and 6 month Silver 3 Month = $312(Adult) + $50 joining fee, $249.60 (Concession) + $50 joining fee Silver 6 Month = $624 (Adult) + $50 joining fee,$499.20 (Concession) + $50 joining fee Gold 3 Month = $572 (Adult) + $50 joining fee, $457.60 (Concession) + $50 joining fee Gold 6 Month = $1144 (Adult) + $50 joining fee, $915.20(Concession) + $50 joining fee Memberships Saturday, October 28, 2023 3:56 PM Recovery at DFC The Danny Frawley Centre’s unique sports Recovery Centre in Moorabbin VIC will service athletes and sports clubs alike with access to high-tech and advanced sports recovery services to improve performance and recovery in individuals. Memberships are now available for purchase as well as casual recovery session bookings. Our memberships start from $44 a week, giving you access to our: Recovery Centre• Aquatics facilities, including our 25m and hydrotherapy pool• Gym & Health Club• Lockers• What is the benefit of each service? Infrared Saunas assist in relieving inflammation, stiffness and soreness by increasing blood circulation and heart rate Normatec Compression Boots aid in recovery by increasing circulation and enhancing lymphatic drainage leading to an increased range of motion and flexibility. Ice baths use reduces the risk of injury and muscle damage from exercise by constricting blood vessels and decreasing metabolic activity. The process speeds up recovery making you better prepared for your next workout allowing you to perform more effectively Hyperice Massage Guns will deliver a massage experience whereby the user can pinpoint the areas of their body that require attention to apply a specific amount of pressure through the gun that will release tension and increase muscle metabolism. What do I need to bring and what do I wear? For all sessions we require patrons to bring a towel and drink bottle to use throughout their time in the recovery space. If you are completing an infrared sauna or ice bath session it is a requirement to wear your bathers in the same way you would in a swimming pool. When using the Normatec compression boots it is a requirement to wear full length pants/leggings underneath the boots. Massage guns can be used through clothing so there are no extra requirements when using these. How long do sessions go for? Each booking is for 45 minutes which includes a quick set up and pack up component to ensure you get the most out of your session. What is the minimum age for use of the Recovery Sessions? Minimum age for use of ice baths and infrared sauna is 16 years of age. Exceptions may apply upon presentation of advice from medical practitioner or allied health professional. Minimum age of use for Hyperice Massage technology and Normatec compression technology is 13 years of age. ### Membership Prices and Options
East Fremantle Membership: The EP membership includes the same Exercise Physiology sessions as individual appointments, but it’s set up as an ongoing program through weekly or fortnightly direct debit. It’s designed for members who need regular, ongoing support rather than one-off sessions. Because it’s a bundled membership, sessions generally can’t be claimed through Medicare, private health, or WorkCover — those rebates usually apply only to individually paid sessions. Members are welcome to check directly with their fund to see if any coverage applies, but in most cases it does not. One condition of this membership is a minimum four-week commitment before switching to another membership type, which helps cover the initial assessment and program setup cost. There is a self service kiosk with hundreds of different classes available, members will be asked to do a virtual induction if they haven't used the reformer beds before. We offer two sessions every hour (as long as the gym is staffed, instances where the gym isn't staffed there will not be any sessions available) between 6.00am and 8.00pm (first booking period is 6.15am-7.00am, last booking period is 7.15pm-8.00pm) Members could theoretically do 3 15-minute classes, or 1 45-minute class. We are allied health professionals who specialise in Exercise to help treat and manage chronic conditions and injuries • What types of exercise? Land/Gym, Hydrotherapy, Home Exercise• Can they help with my injuries and conditions? - YES, most will benefit from exercise, refer to our website • What types of consultations do we offer? - Initial Assessment (60mins), Follow up (30-60mins), Group Sessions (60mins) • Can my third-party payer cover this cost? - YES, in most circumstances, please refer below for the specific scheme. We offer Medicare, DVA, TAC, WorkSafe, NDIS, Private Health and My Aged Care. • Is Exercise Physiology included in my Gurri Membership? Is this service complimentary? - NO – this is a separate service to the facility, and requires extra cost involved. Third party schemes may assist in covering part of the cost. • What if I am not a member of Gurri, can I still access this service and use the facility to exercise? - YES & NO – Clients require an appointment either 1:1 or Group session to access the facility. The client can also pay ‘casually entry’/’per session’ basis. • If in doubt, please refer to the website for all the details as we try and keep this updated. If you are unsure, please refer the client/enquirer to our website for information and offer the Allied Health email. gwwcalliedhealth@belgravialeisure.com.au EXERCISE PHYSIOLOGY Monday, 18 November 2024 12:39 PM No referral necessary to seek treatment• Gym or Hydro sessions – frequency depending on the amount of funding available• More information on website to refer to• No gap payment required from client – NDIS funding full amount• Private Health Insurance Current timetable will be on website: Group Fitness - Gurri Wanyarra Wellbeing Centre (gurriwanyarrawc.com.au) Over 100 classes per week (including Reformer Pilates)• Bookings essential via Active World• Only class that does not require bookings is All Abilities Dance, which can be paid casually at reception. • Group Fitness Thursday, December 01, 2022 4:55 PM PT Prices 60 min - $76.60 30 min - $52.50 Process for booking PT is via website enquiry. Often, this will be in a follow up appointment. • What happens in an appointment? - EP talks with client about medical history, goals, exercise history etc. Complete some tests/assessment to determine appropriateness/safety for exercise. Sometimes we can complete some exercise prescription at the end of the session. • Follow up: 30-60mins Client must have completed an initial appointment before commencing ongoing exercise, if it has been longer than >3-6 months since they have seen us, it is likely they will need to be reassessed • Gym, Hydrotherapy or Home Exercise Program• Groups: up to 60mins We have Hydrotherapy Group and Gym Group (EP Hour). ### Opening Hours
Gympie Opening Hours: Our centre contains a 25m indoor heated pool, gym, cafe and childrens splash park that are open year round. We also have a seasonal 50m outdoor pool and double waterslides. Check the hours for each attraction below. Gym Open Hours Our gym is inside our centre, and open during general centre hours. Splash Park Monday to Thursday: 9:00am to 5:00pm Friday to Sunday: 9:00am to 4:00pm Public Holidays: 9:00am to 4:00pm Waterslides Our large waterslides are seasonal. They are open from the start of Term 3 school holidays in September, until the end of the Term 1 school holidays in April. Please note: Riders must be a minimum of 1.2 metres tall and at least 6 years old. Waterslide armbands are an additional cost to general entry and offer unlimited rides on the day of purchase. Weekdays During School Terms: Closed Saturday and Sunday: 10:30am to 3:30pm (seasonal) School Holidays Daily: 10:30am - 3:30pm (seasonal) Public Holidays: 10:30am - 3:30pm (seasonal) Cafe Cold drinks and packaged food such as ice-creams and sandwiches etc can be purchased at any time during open hours. Our kiosk is currently operating a 'grab and go' menu, with fresh food available thoughout the day for purchase. Hot chips are available between 9am and 3pm daily. Group Fitness Our current group fitness timetables can be found under 'Swim' for aqua session or 'Train' for land based group fitness. Squad Training Our squad training timetable can be found under our 'Swim' tab, on our squad page. Facility Tuesday, 10 December 2024 10:53 AM Monday to Thursday 5.30 am to 8:00 pm Friday 5.30 am to 7:00 pm Saturday 6.00 am to 5.00 pm Sunday 8.00 am to 5.00 pm Public holidays 8.00 am to 5.00 pm Closed Good Friday and Christmas Day• Anzac Day open from 1pm to 5pm • 50m outdoor (unheated) pool and large waterslides are open seasonally from the start of term 3 school holidays until the end of term 1 school holidays. • www.gympiearc.com.au/venue/hours Outdoor pool closed from Tuesday 22nd April Kids Play area currently undergoing renovations: At least another week until its done• Check socials for updates on when its up&running again• (as of 20/09/2025) Opening Hours Monday, April 15, 2024 5:05 PM Joining Fee: $60.00 One Off 2025 /2026 SQUAD teachers Taylah is the morning coach and I am the afternoon coach. Address: 29 Service Road Melbourne Airport VIC 3045 WHERE TO FIND US Higher State is located within the brand-new Novotel and ibis Styles Hotel, just a five-minute walk from Terminal 4 at Melbourne Airport. We are conveniently located just past Terminal 4 car park, ride share pick up/drop off and bus interchange. Main member entrance from Service Road. For new members or casual entry, please visit Novotel reception to gain access, or see staff at Higher State by calling or ringing the doorbell. FOR GUESTS THAT HAVE TROUBLE FINDING US For guests that have trouble finding us, advise them to drive past the main entrance of the Novotel/Ibis Styles hotel on Grants road and take a left at the traffic lights. Parking is located about 50m up the road, and guests can take a left to enter the underground carpark. Please note the carpark is owned and managed by Accor, and parking there is at an hourly rate unless they have a parking membership (See Parking Info tab). ### Casual Entry and Visit Passes
Higher State Melb Airport Casual rates: Fitness Passport is accepted for entry to Higher State. Irregular/Once off Casual Use – Fitness Passport members to arrive during staffed hours (6am-8pm) and have a staff member let them in. For casual access on an irregular basis, FP members should scan the QR code located in the lobby. Regular use (At least once per week) - Speak to a staff member to register on ActiveWorld as a Fitness Passport member. An access card will be provided (allow 2-3 business days to set up), and the member will no longer have to scan the QR code on each visit, and can visit the gym 24/7. ## Keilor East Leisure Centre

### Contact Information
Keilor East Leisure Centre Contact Information: Website https://www.movemv.com.au/keilor-east-leisure-centre/ Venue Manager – James Worboyes Aquatic Services Manager – Mylene Nguyen Vo Aquatic Services Coordinator – Matthew Arrowsmith Health Club Manager – Adrian Mott Health Club Coordinator – Kasey Pisani Operations Manager – Julian Valentino Operations Coordinator – Brandon White Sales and Guest Experience Manager – Gulsen Krastic Sales and Guest Experience Coordinator – Molly Tyrell Address: 84 Quinn Grove, Keilor East Leisure, 3033 Ph: 9283 6402 Email: kelcinfo@movemv.com.au Website: www.movemv.com.au Contact info and Staff Friday, June 20, 2025 4:54 PM Classes are led by qualified Reformer Pilates instructors with additional postpartum Pilates training. Please note: staff should always remind participants to refer to their doctor if unsure about their readiness to participate. 13. What if a participant misses a class? Missed classes are not refundable or transferable unless prior arrangements are made. Encourage mums to attend consistently to gain full benefits. Why? This is a 6-week block program, with the next block commencing immediately after the current one finishes. • In some cases, we may run two concurrent 6-week blocks at different times/days. If a participant knows in advance they’ll miss a class, they should contact the centre ASAP to check if a place is available in an alternative block. • • 14. What if a participant has special concerns (e.g. abdominal separation, prolapse, or pain)? The EOI form captures details about delivery, abdominal separation, pelvic floor concerns, and other medical conditions. If flagged, staff should inform the instructor prior to the first session so modifications can be made. • Always remind participants that they should stop if they feel pain and check back with their health professional. • • 15. MOVE is committed to making sure access to insurance and rehabilitation memberships is a simple and easy process for all. MOVE works with many insurers to streamline the application and payment system for you, so once you have your insurance claim approved, you can join and start your rehabilitation activities. Your insurance and rehabilitation membership can be used for a variety of activities such as warm water physical therapy, lap swimming, gym work and exercise physiologists. Speak to your health professional about what therapy you require. MOVE work with many insurance agencies including; the Transport Accident Commission (TAC), Gallagher Bassett, GIO, EML, and Workcover, just to name a few. Process: Send email to customer with Insurance Membership Quote attached and request an approval letter from their insurance provider. Insurance Quotes 1. Once we receive approval letter, we process the membership and send invoice to Provider to pay and email to customer to notify their membership is now active and ready to use. (They don't need to wait for the invoice to be paid first – membership can start straight away). 2. Baby & Me Reformer –Staff FAQ 1. What is the Baby & Me Reformer program? Baby & Me Reformer is a six-week, post-natal Pilates program designed to help new mums safely return to exercise after birth. Sessions focus on core and pelvic floor activation, posture, mobility, and overall wellbeing, all while connecting with baby. 2. Who can join the program? Mums with babies from 6 weeks postpartum to 9 months (ideally not yet crawling).• Medical clearance is required prior to participating.• • 3. Is medical clearance required? Yes. All participants must provide medical clearance from a healthcare provider before starting the program, regardless of delivery type. 4. How long is the program and what is the structure? Duration: 6 weeks• Session length: 45 minutes• Small group setting: max. 4 participants per class (ensuring individual attention).• • 5. How much does it cost? The program is priced at $207 for six weeks, payable in full before the first session. 6. How do I purchase and book? A “Reformer. Baby and Me” 6 Visit Pass is available on Active World.• If the participant doesn’t already have an AW account, please create one for the participant before purchasing. • Baby and Me Reformer Pilates - Relaunch Thursday, September 04, 2025 1:48 PM Holiday Program: GOswim Active World Holiday Program Demo 2025 Summer Holiday Swimming Program Attend our 5-day holiday program to continue progressing over the summer. With the philosophy of exercise is medicine, our membership program provides an individual tailored exercise treatment plan for everyone who joins. We firmly believe that a ‘one size fits all’ approach does not work when managing illnesses and injuries. We take into account your specific health concerns, needs and goals and apply an evidence-based approach to treatment in a socially welcoming approach. With our Exercise Physiology Group Program, you’ll enjoy: Personalised exercise plans designed by our Exercise Physiologists• Access to a dedicated Exercise Physiology Group timetable with Gym, Hydrotherapy and Reformer classes led by our Exercise Physiology team. • Initial Assessment and Quarterly progress and program reviews to keep you on track• Full membership access to the venue to use anytime.• Along with all the benefits of our MOVE Gold membership, which includes Full Facility Access (Aquatic and Health Club areas), Group Fitness classes, Reformer Pilates and B Active Functional Training classes. ### Membership Prices and Options
Keilor East Leisure Centre Membership: before purchasing. To book the client into their sessions, follow this path within the ‘Book Session’ page: Activity → Group Fitness → Program → Reformer Pilates → Level → Reformer Mums and Bubs. • Staff must book the client into all 6 classes (one at a time).• • 7. Can mums bring their baby into the class? Yes. Babies stay close by, either in their pram or on a mat next to mum. The class is designed to be inclusive and safe for both mum and baby. 8. What is the difference between regular Reformer classes and Baby & Me Reformer? Regular Reformer classes are open to the general population and focus on fitness, mobility, and strength. Baby & Me Reformer is specifically designed for postpartum mums, with exercises modified for safe return to movement, pelvic floor and core rehabilitation, and baby-inclusive participation. 9. Is this program included in my membership? No, this program is not included in standard membership. However, you don’t need to be a member to participate — it is open to all eligible mums. 10. How do I purchase and book? A “Reformer. Medical clearance letter prior to first session (if not already provided).• Comfortable workout clothes.• Baby’s essentials (pram, blanket, toys, nappies).• Water bottle and towel.• • 12. The VIC Government is offering $200 rebates parents can redeem towards our programs (such as Swimming Lessons!) You can use this voucher towards the following programs in centre: GOswim Swimming Lessons• Squads• Teen Gym / Active• How to claim your voucher: Step 1: Ensure you and your child meet the voucher criteria Step 2: Enrol or Register into an eligible program offered at our Facility Step 3: Apply for a voucher (https://www.getactive.vic.gov.au/vouchers/apply-for- vouchers/) Step 4: Select Belgravia Health and Leisure as your provider Step 5: Give your voucher to one of our friendly Customer Service staff members Remember: You will need to complete a separate application for each child per rebate.• You can only apply for 1 rebate per child per claim period and up to two vouchers for each eligible child up to 30 April 2024. • You can be reimbursed for an amount above $50 and up to $200 per eligible child. If your program registration cost is $100, you will only be reimbursed $100 not the total $200. • Get Active Kids Voucher Friday, June 27, 2025 10:40 AM

### Exercise Physiology
Keilor East Leisure Centre Exercise Physiology: MOVE Moonee Valley's accredited exercise physiologists deliver you safe and effective exercise interventions to help you reach your optimal health. Accredited exercise physiologists (AEPs) are university qualified, allied health professionals with the knowledge, skills and competencies to serve those with acute, sub-acute or chronic medical conditions, injuries or disabilities. If you have Private Health insurance or you're currently under WorkCover, TAC, DVA or NDIS funding streams you may qualify for rebates under these compensable schemes. Pathology domains covered by the services of AEPs include: Kidney Cancers Metabolic Neurological Cardiovascular Musculoskeletal Respiratory/pulmonary and mental health Any other conditions for which there is evidence that exercise can improve the client’s clinical status. Exercise Physiology appointments made online via link below: Nookal - Online Bookings For more information about Exercise Physiology services and to book an initial consultation, customers can fill in and submit the below online form: Exercise Physiology Expression of Interest Form (KELC) Exercise Physiology Thursday, June 26, 2025 5:01 PM MOVE Moonee Valley's accredited exercise physiologists deliver you safe and effective exercise interventions to help you reach your optimal health. Accredited exercise physiologists (AEPs) are university qualified, allied health professionals with the knowledge, skills and competencies to serve those with acute, sub-acute or chronic medical conditions, injuries or disabilities. If you have Private Health insurance or you're currently under WorkCover, TAC, DVA or NDIS funding streams you may qualify for rebates under these compensable schemes. Pathology domains covered by the services of AEPs include: Kidney Cancers Metabolic Neurological Cardiovascular Musculoskeletal Respiratory/pulmonary and mental health Any other conditions for which there is evidence that exercise can improve the client’s clinical status.

Swim School Tuesday, December 20, 2022 5:02 PM QUESTION ANSWER What is the App? The App is the parent-facing component of Active World. Parents will be able to download the app from the Apple store or Google Play Store. The app will allow users to: Book students• Manage their profile for themselves and their children• Manage their billing details• View their payment history• Communicate with Centre staff• Advise Centre of non-attendance• See a live schedule of student classes that is individual to the parent’s profile • Track skills and progression to date and what else needs to be done to keep achieving • I don’t have an iPhone. Can I download to an android device? Yes, the app can be downloaded through your app store. Just search for ActiveWorld. You can also use the URL provided to login on any device A student is missing from a family, how do I get them added ? If your child is not enrolled, you can simply add them as a member to your profile via your app. Can multiple parents/guardians have the app and view progression information ? Yes, multiple parents/guardians can see progress information. You can add the new person to your profile as a Relative. Once you added to your profile, the relative can download the app onto their phone and login using the same information on the customer profile. They will be able to see everything expect personal details and account information. I didn’t receive the Welcome e-mail Check your junk inbox If nothing has been received check your email information with the Centre. My email address has changed, how do I update it? Login to your app and update your email address on your personal profile page How do I log in? Use the email you signed up with Download the App or log into the portal using the e-mail address provided. Use Knox as the code then use the email you signed up with, select forgot password and an email will be sent to create a new password. QUESTION ANSWER Is the App Free? Yes What if my child can’t attend a class ? There’s no need to contact us if your child will be absent from their lesson. Simply go to the Active World app at least two hours before your class starts and select that your child will be absent from their lesson. You have 6 make-up lessons a year. If you put your absence in at least two hours before your class starts you will automatically receive a make-up class from what is available, which you can book in yourself using the app, at your convenience. The make-up class remains on the system for 14 days. What if I need to suspend my child’s lessons? If you know in advance you will be absent from a class for up to two weeks (e.g. going on holiday) you can suspend your lesson. This means that you will not be charged for the lesson, but will be charged a $5 fee to retain your spot in your class and will not receive a makeup class. You can suspend on the app. Please contact info@knoxleisureworks.com.au to discuss this. How do I opt out of classes? Your classes will be ongoing until you let us know you wish to cancel. There is a 30 day cancellation time, in which lessons can be attended as normal. Please email info@knoxleisurworks.com.au to cancel or ask for a form at the customer service desk. How often does my child get assessed? The children are being assessed constantly as all children progress in their own way and their own time. The APP is a good indicator of the skills that have been achieved as well as their progression along the way. How to change classes? On the APP, Go into manage account and change class. If you need to change level as your child has been promoted; speak to the ASO on pool deck or at the customer service desk. Cryo Lounge- new Monday, October 27, 2025 1:22 PM CHILD CARE CHANGES Hi Everyone, Hopefully it doesn't get to you, but just advising you that there will be some communications going to 37 families today, around upcoming changes to the childcare. Effective July 1 2024, we will be permanently closing our childcare facilities at Knox Leisureworks. This decision has not been made lightly where careful analysis around where the leisure industry is and the rising costs associated in operating sessional childcare. The following communications will go to 37 families that have utilised the childcare in 2024 at 9:30am this morning. Please refrain from mentioning the closure before then and if any media enquiries contact Knox Leisureworks for comment, please advise "no comment" and to grab their details and send to me, for correct response from our media response team. Subject: Changes in Child Care Services at Knox Leisureworks. Dear (member name), We wish to inform our members and community members that from July 1 2024 we will be closing our Child Care services at Knox Leisureworks. This has been a difficult decision that we have have delayed as long as possible. We understand this will impact some of the families in our community, particularly on those parents and guardians who rely on Knox Leisureworks child care as part of their health & wellbeing activities. However, despite our best efforts to sustain and retain these services, we have faced changes in the industry and increasing challenges to fund the service that have led to the conclusion that continuing the childcare is no longer feasible. Effective July 1 2024, the childcare services at Knox Leisureworks will cease operations permanently. We are committed to assisting our members during this transition period and will provide information regarding alternative childcare options in the local area. We remain dedicated to providing the best possible services in all areas of Knox Leisureworks and look forward to continuing to serve you in those capacities. Kind Regards, Knox Leisureworks FAQ's - Will my membership get cheaper? Platinum memberships will be reduced in price effective July 1. Since November 2022, new members have not received child care as a part of their membership benefits. As of 01/07/2024 childcare is no longer available Childcare Tuesday, December 20, 2022 5:03 PM Hoist is available for the warm water pool. Wheel chair access Tuesday, November 04, 2025 2:28 PM

### Membership Prices and Options

Each family member with the membership gets the discounted rate. A parent can also get the family rate if they have a child enrolled in swimming lessons. Whereas Salary Sacrifice does not, despite offering the same income to our centre). Trials Thursday, April 20, 2023 12:39 PM FILL IN MEDICAL FORM Did they tick YES ??? - MUST GET A MEDICAL CLEARANCE BEFORE BOOKING IN • Confirm they have filled in all details before booking them • BOOK INTO CLASS Make sure the class has an instructor (if it doesn't, don't book & message Kai)• Appointment 1 - Beginning (Day 1- 3 of membership) From the Beginning we will take the time to understand your goals, your motivations and your reasons to change. We will build a baseline to measure and map your progress and develop a personalised gym program designed and demonstrated to you. Appointment 2 - Check-In (Day 14 -17 of membership) Your Check-In is the appointment which will take place approximately two weeks after your Beginning appointment. Here, we will focus on how you are finding your personalised program and where we can make any changes to ensure you’re on the right track. Appointment 3 - Benefits (Day 30 of membership) In your third appointment, we will re-visit your Beginning baseline markers and review how we have progressed in the initial 30 days and the Benefits you have gained. Your trainer can change up your program at this time and provide guidance on your next steps with assisted or accelerated training programs. WHO NEEDS A BEGIN ACTIVE ADULTS• TEENS • BEGIN Wednesday, February 21, 2024 8:02 PM Aquacise (regular): In 50m pool • 1 hour session • Included in AA, aquatic, platinum and wellness memberships • Casual entry is $18.10 or $15.60 with concession• Low impact workout • Gentle aquacise: In warm water pool• More beginner/elderly/injury friendly• 1 hour session• Aqua Flow * In Warm Water Pool Warm water pool – up to 1.6m deep Aquatic Group Exercise Classes Friday, September 8, 2023 2:55 PM received child care as a part of their membership benefits. Why is it closing? Across the Health and Wellness industry, many large facilities are ceasing child care due to increasing costs, decreasing participation and changes in the industry towards using the facility for other activity. Whats happening to the staff? We are working with the staff to help find alternate work, duties and employment opportunities. Our child care team are a small but important part of the wider team, we know this is a big impact for them and we’ll do our best to support them through it. Who made this decision? The management company, Belgravia Leisure has led this change. This change has been accepted by the owners of Knox Leisureworks - Knox City Council. What sort of membership are Knox Council Members eligible for? All Membership Types at 50% off. (except wellness) Refer to: Discounted Membership Options for more info. NDIS- Invoices for memberships or passes cannot be invoiced by us, they have to get funded through NDIS first, then come through to Knox and pay like a normal pass and/or membership. ### Location and Access

Payments As consideration for receipt of the Services, the Customer agrees to pay the instalment amount at the agreed payment frequency for the term of this Contract. The Customer authorises Debitsuccess to add any fees owing under this clause to any future instalments paid by the Customer (as a separate payment or otherwise). 9. Privacy The Customer acknowledges that: Debitsuccess is entitled to store his or her personal information (whether received from the Customer, the Facility or otherwise) on its systems, and use it for the purposes of administering this Contract, providing its products and services, or offering alternative products and services; he or she has rights of access to, and correction of, his or her information under the Privacy Act 1988 (Cth); and Debitsuccess (or the Facility) may contact the Customer for any purpose related to the provision of its products and services. 10. Liability The Customer agrees that, to the extent permitted by law, neither the Facility, Debitsuccess or any of their related companies, directors or employees will be liable for any direct, indirect, or consequential injury, loss or damage to the Customer, or to the property of the Customer whatsoever, arising out of or in relation to this Contract. 11. Debt Collection Action The Customer: authorises the Debitsuccess to notify any debt collection or credit reporting agency upon default by the Customer in regard to any obligation to pay under this Contract; ○ agrees to immediately pay the full outstanding balance of the remainder of the payments due, including any current arrears, should a default occur prior to this Contract terminating; ○ authorises Debitsuccess to add $50 to the outstanding debt as its fee for dealing with the default; and ○ agrees to pay any and all costs incurred as a result of debt collection including the commission, fees and costs charged by any debt collection agency (approximately 25% of the outstanding debt). ○ 12. Contracts Privity The Customer acknowledges that Debitsuccess has been contracted by the Facility to collect the instalments due under this Contract and the Customer acknowledges that all rights of the Facility pursuant to this Contract are able to be enforced by Debitsuccess as if it were the Facility, without any involvement on the part of the Facility or the consent of the Customer. 13. Entire Agreement This Contract and the Facility Membership Agreement (as applicable) constitutes the entire agreement, understanding and arrangement (express and implied) between the Customer, the Facility and Debitsuccess relating to the subject matter of this Contract, and supersedes and cancels any previous agreement, understanding and arrangement relating to the subject matter of these arrangements whether written or oral. In the event of any inconsistency between the terms of this Contract and the Facility Membership Agreement that specifically relate to the rights and obligations of the Facility (other than any right to unilaterally vary fees payable), the terms of the Facility Membership Agreement shall prevail. 14. Severability If any provision of this Contract is prohibited, invalid or unenforceable, that provision will be ineffective to the extent of the prohibition, invalidity or unenforceability without invalidating the remaining provisions of this Contract or affecting the validity or enforceability of that provision, unless it materially alters the nature or material terms of this Contract. TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF THE DEBITSUCCESS DIRECT DEBIT REQUEST (DDR) SERVICE AGREEMENT 1. INITIAL TERMS Debitsuccess will debit your nominated account for the amounts and at the frequency of payments as agreed between us on the Debitsuccess DDR Contract, authorised and accepted by you. THE PRODUCT The Product is a non-cash payment facility which allows you to enter into an arrangement with us for the payment of reoccurring amounts to a single merchant by direct debit from your nominated bank account or credit card ('Account'). We can only provide the facility to you if we have received a completed Direct Debit Request that you have agreed to. UPDATED INFORMATION Some information might change from time to time. We will issue a supplementary or replacement Short-Form PDS to you if there is a materially adverse change to or omission from the information. For other changes, you can obtain up to date information by contacting us. We will send you updated Information free of charge on request. DISCLAIMER All information in this Short-Form PDS is general only and does not take account of your individual objectives, financial situation or specific needs. You should consider how the information in this Short-Form PDS meets your needs before deciding to apply for the Product. OTHER INFORMATION THAT FORMS PART OF THIS SHORT-FORM PDS The following documents are incorporated into, and form part of, this Short-Form PDS: 1. The Terms and Conditions of the Debitsuccess Contract and/or your customer/service contract; and 2.The Terms and Conditions of the Debitsuccess Direct Debit Request (DDR) Service Agreement. You should read these documents as they include important information about the terms and conditions that apply to our provision of the Product to you, including information about cancellation and termination rights, breach of contract, liability and privacy. They are printed on the back of our Direct Debit Request (DDR) which you will be given by the merchant you require your payment to be made to. The documents are also publically available to view or download from our website or you can ask us for a copy. SUMMARY OF FEATURES AND BENEFITS OF THE PRODUCT The Product allows you to make recurring payments from your Account to a single merchant - for example a club or organisation you have membership to. It has many benefits, the key ones are summarised below: Certainty - you can align payments to your income stream by nominating the day payments are to be deducted from your Account and the frequency. Flexibility - nominate payments to continue or stop on expiry of the minimum term. Responsiveness - you can elect to pay more over a shorter term (paying off your liability earlier) or if your circumstances change you can arrange to make 'catch-up' payments in special circumstances. Security of Data - we have in place security systems of a very high standard which comply with the Payment Card Industry Data Security Standards to ensure that your personal information is secure from unauthorised access. SUMMARY OF RISKS OF USING THE PRODUCT The Product is designed to provide you with a simple and easy to use payment solution. The Product is not 100% risk free and there are some risks associated with use of the Product. We cannot debit your account if you give us incorrect Account Detail or if you have insufficient clear funds in your Account and in the unlikely event that our systems or service providers are temporarily unavailable we may not be able to debit your Account on the nominated day. DISPUTE RESOLUTION If you are not satisfied with our services, please telephone our internal dispute resolution service on 1800 148 848 or write to us. We will acknowledge your complaint in writing within 7 days and endeavour to resolve it promptly. If you are not satisfied with our response, we are a member of the Financial Ombudsman Service, an external dispute resolution body who you can contact by telephone (1300 780 808), fax (03 9613 6399), in writing (GPO Box 3, Melbourne VIC 3001) or via their website (www.fos.org.au). COSTS AND OTHER AMOUNTS PAYABLE We may deduct the following fees from your Account at the times indicated: Fee Amount When Payable Administ ration* A maximum amount of $110. The fee could range between $0 and $110 depending on your arrangement with your merchant For example: You may be charged a one off fee of $10 if so it will be clearly indicated on the DDR form that you complete with your merchant Once only when Product is first established Reversal Up to $15 On the Dishonour of a payment Debt Collectio n** $50 plus 25% of full outstanding balance. For example, if your outstanding balance was $200, the Debt Cancellation Fee owing, in addition to the outstanding contract balance of $200, will be $100 (comprising $50 plus 25% of the remaining balance (i.e. 25% of $200). On cancellation of the product due to your failure to pay the required amounts under your customer/membership contract resulting in the referral of your account to Debt Collection. *The fees noted in the table above are maximum amounts charged by Debitsuccess in relation to the provision of the product. The actual amounts payable are set out in your customer/membership contract. You will be notified in writing of the amount you pay

CHANGE OF TERMS In the unlikely event that the initial terms are to change, they can only do so in accordance wit your Contract and we ust ive you at least 14 days’ notice of t e changes including if applicable the new amount, new frequency and next debit date. 3. DEFERRING OR STOPPING A PAYMENT Should you wish to defer a payment to another date you must contact Debitsuccess before the date of that payment to request the deferment. Deferments are entirely at the discretion of Debitsuccess and will depend on the length of deferment, the current state of your account and your past history. You may request us to stop an individual payment however you will still be liable to make this payment by some other method or your account will become overdue 4. ALTERING THE SCHEDULE Should you wish to alter the payment frequency or Day to Debit, contact Debitsuccess and we, at our discretion, may be able to make the changes you require. There may be a fee charged for this service (details of any fees payable can be obtained by contacting Debitsuccess on 1-800 148 848). Any changes made will not affect the total amount you would otherwise have paid over the minimum term of your Contract. 5. SUSPENDING THE PAYMENTS Suspension of payments may be possible under the terms of your Facility Membership Agreement. Payments may be suspended for a minimum of 2 weeks at a time so long as the total time suspended within the minimum term does not exceed 6 weeks. In order to suspend payments you should contact Debitsuccess at least 3 days prior to the date of the first suspended payment. There is a charge of $5.00 per week while the contract is suspended unless a different fee is specified on the front of this Contract. Any time spent on suspension will be added onto the minimum term of the Contract so that the sum of the instalments payable for the minimum term or number of payments shall still be payable regardless of any suspension or suspension charges made. 6. CANCELLING THE PAYMENTS You can cancel this Direct Debit Request Authority by requesting this of Debitsuccess or your bank. Cancellation of the authority to debit your account will not terminate this contract or remove your liability to make the payments you have agreed to. 7. DISPUTES If you dispute any debit payment, you must notify Debitsuccess immediately. Debitsuccess will respond to your dispute within 7 working days and will immediately refund the amount of the debit if we are not able to substantiate the reason for it. If you do not receive a satisfactory response from us to your dispute contact your financial institution who will respond to you with an answer to your claim within 5 business days if your claim is lodged within 12 months of the disputed drawing, or within 30 business days if your claim is lodged after 12 months from the disputed drawing. 8. NON WORKING DAY When the day to debit falls on a weekend or public holiday the debit will be initiated on the next working day. 9. DISHONOURED PAYMENTS It is your responsibility to ensure that on the due date clear funds are available in your nominated account to meet the direct debit payment. Should your payment be dishonoured, Debitsuccess will debit the amount indicated on the front of this Contract with your next payment and may, if we have not received instructions to the contrary from you, debit both the current due payment and the now overdue payment(s) on the same day. Debitsuccess may debit other fees or costs involved with debt collection in accordance with the terms and conditions of the Contract. 10. ENQUIRIES All enquiries should be directed to Debitsuccess and should be made at least 1 working day prior to the next scheduled debit date. 11. YOUR OTHER RESPONSIBILITIES In addition to those already mentioned, you are responsible for ensuring that your nominated account is able to accept direct debits. If it is not, it is your responsibility to provide Debitsuccess with a new account number. ### Group Fitness
Mill Park Group Fitness: Booking & Payment Please download the Active World App, and create a customer profile. Note: The Centre must be set to Mill Park Leisure. This can be change via 'My Profile' if you already have an existing account. Steps to book into the School Holiday Sessions: Press 'Book Group Fitness'1. Press the magnifying glass icon (right hand side)2. Change the Activity to 'Children's Programs' (tap the blue arrow for the drop down options) 3. All other filters do not need to be changed4. Press 'Search'5. Press 'Book' next to your desired session day/time6. Press 'Continue'7. Select 'Add Member' (fill out your child's details - please ensure the Photo Consent and Medical Conditions incl. allergies are filled out at this step) 8. Press 'Add'9. Select the Member Name (child's name - using the blue arrow)10. Press 'Continue'11. Press 'Confirm Booking'12. Enter card details to make payment13. Press '$20.00' to confirm and process payment14. The steps above will have to be repeated per session and/or per child. Bookings are not confirmed until payment has been received. Terms & Conditions When booking into these sessions via the Active World App, you are agreeing to the following: · Children must be primary school ages (5-12 years) · Price = $20/session · Dietary requirements must be advised prior · Medical conditions must be advised prior · Payment upfront to secure spot · Non-refundable event

### Exercise Physiology
Mill Park Exercise Physiology: Reach optimal health with exercise physiology Accredited Exercise Physiologists (AEPs) are university qualified allied health professionals equipped with the knowledge, skills and competencies to design, deliver and evaluate safe and effective exercise interventions. Now offering one hour one-on-one hydrotherapy sessions with an exercise physiologoist. Exercise physiology is for people with acute, sub-acute or chronic medical conditions, injuries or disabilities. Pathology domains covered by the services of AEPs include: NDIS Kidney Cancers Metabolic Neurological Cardiovascular Musculoskeletal Respiratory/pulmonary and mental health Any other conditions for which there is evidence that exercise can improve the client’s clinical status. If you have Private Health insurance or you are currently under WorkCover, TAC, DVA funding streams you may qualify for rebates under these compensable schemes. INTERESTED IN EXERCISE PHYSIOLOGY? CLICK HERE TO ENQUIRE NOW. Exercise Physiology Friday, April 12, 2024 10:01 AM

Monbulk Opening Hours: Hours of Operation: Monbulk Aquatic Centre Trading Hours Monday - Friday Gym Only 5.30am - 9pm; Centre 6am - 9pm (pool closes at 8.30pm)• Saturday & Sunday 8am - 6pm (pool closes at 5.45pm)• Public Holidays as per weekend hours• Group Fitness Timetables may vary during School holidays and on Public Holidays• All patrons, please note between 6pm and 6.30pm weekdays, lap swimming lanes are not available. Grand Final Public Holiday Trading Hours: Friday 26th September 8.00am - 6.00pm• GOswim classes operate as per normal EXCEPT for the 5.45pm classes will not run and members will not be charged for this class. • Group Fitness Timetable for Grand Final Public Holiday : Please see ActiveWorld for accurate class times. Instagram and Facebook also have posts with images of the temporary timetable during the public holiday. • Opening Hours & Grand Final Public Holiday Trading Thursday, December 01, 2022 12:43 PM If your child is unable to attend a scheduled GOswim class, you may be eligible to book a make-up lesson. Here's how it works: ✅How to Arrange a Make-Up Lesson Log the absence via the ActiveWorld App at least 24 hours before the class.• Once logged, you’ll have 14 days to book and attend a make-up lesson.• Annual Allowance Each GOswim student is entitled to up to 6 make-up lessons per calendar year.• Make-up lessons are subject to class availability and occupancy.• If You're Within 24 Hours of the Class If you're unable to log the absence in the app (less than 24 hours before class), please call Reception on (03) 9756 8000 within 2 hours of the scheduled class time. • A minimum 2-hour notice is required to allow for staffing and space planning.• Rebooking a Make-Up Once a make-up lesson is booked, it can only be rescheduled within the original 14- day window from the date of the missed class. • Make-Up Classes Monday, September 01, 2025 11:21 AM As an approved Get Active Kids VIC provider, we’re making it easier for kids to get active! The VIC Government is offering $200 rebates parents can redeem towards our programs (such as Swimming Lessons!) You can use this voucher towards the following programs in centre: GOswim Swimming Lessons• Squads• Teen Gym / Active• How to claim your voucher: Step 1: Ensure you and your child meet the voucher criteria Step 2: Enrol or Register into an eligible program offered at our Facility Step 3: Apply for a voucher (https://www.getactive.vic.gov.au/vouchers/apply-for- vouchers/) Step 4: Select Belgravia Health and Leisure as your provider Step 5: Give your voucher to one of our friendly Customer Service staff members Remember: You will need to complete a separate application for each child per rebate.• You can only apply for 1 rebate per child per claim period and up to two vouchers for each eligible child up to 30 April 2025. • You can be reimbursed for an amount above $50 and up to $200 per eligible child. ### Contact Information
Pelican Park Contact Information: Website https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/ Phone Number: 1300 8727 8980 Email Address: pelicanpark@belgravialeisure.com.au Facility Manager: Judi De La Haye – jdelahaye@belgravialeisure.com.au Assistant Centre Manager/ Operations Manager: Brad Kellett – bkellett@belgravialeisure.com.au Customer Service Coordinators: Eilidh Dorrington – edorrington@belgravialeisure.com Swim School Coordinator: Meredith Wardlaw – mwardlaw@belgravialeisure.com.au Health Club Coordinator: Melissa Bartlett – mbartlett@belgravialeisure.com.au Contact Info Wednesday, December 21, 2022 1:20 PM Personal Training prices: Member Non-Member 30 mins, 1:1 $48.2 $50.60 60 mins, 1:1 $96.4 $101.20 3 x 30 Minute Starter $99.00 $199.00 To organise PT please direct email enquiries to mbartlett@belgravialeisure.com.au Personal Training Wednesday, December 21, 2022 1:21 PM How do I cancel my membership? Cancellation Requests All membership cancellations are done via the Cancellation Request forms on our website under the Contact Us section: https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/contact- us/membership-portal Members also have the option of suspending their membership as an alternative. All direct debit members can suspend their membership via their Activeworld Membership Management App. Minimum suspension period is 2 weeks up to a maximum of 6 week blocks at a time • There are no maximum number of suspensions• Requests to suspend must be submitted at least 3 days prior to the suspension start date • Suspensions incur a weekly cost of $5.00• Memberships cannot be cancelled while on suspension or suspended pending cancellation • Suspending for a longer period. Suspension extension requests can be made in writing to pelicanpark@belgravialeisure.com.au with your suspension reason and period required. The following reasons will be considered with supporting documentation. Please note a suspension end date is required. Medical • Extended Travel• Extenuating Circumstances• Please note there is a 30 day notification period for cancellations and a joining fee will be applicable to new and returning members if it has been more than 6 weeks since they held an active membership. $10 for memberships and $10 for GOswim lessons. Are there reciprocal rights with other Mornington Peninsula Leisure facilities? Yes, depending on your membership type you may have access to our other facilities. To find out if your membership gives you access to our other facilities, call us on 1300 850 197 or get in touch. FAQ Sunday, February 05, 2023 7:35 PM What parking facilities are available? Pelican Park Recreation Centre is located on the Hastings Foreshore. Bitumen & gravel parking is available. As well as accessible parking which is located to the right of the centre's main entrance. Please note that the parking is shared with other users of the Hastings Foreshore. Do we run private lessons for LTS? Yes we do – these need to be organised directly with Meredith mwardlaw@belgravialeisure.com.au Do we offer funded memberships? Yes we do – we charge $470 for 3 months and require an approval letter to generate an invoice, contact edorrington@belgravialeisure.com.au

Compression Boots• Massage Chairs• Ice Bath How to use the Ice Baths: If you have any Health Conditions it is strongly recommended you see a health practitioner prior to first use. 1. Please bring the following items with you – bathers, towel, change of clothes2. All users must shower prior to use of the ice bath3. Safely step into the bath using the support rails to assist participant entry4. Slowly enter ice bath as to manage the stock response to the body, only submerge more of your body in the ice bath as the participant can manage the Synetic nervous system (Fight or Flight response) 5. When exiting the Ice Bath, please slowly and safely exit the bath with the assistance of the safety rails. 6. Once safely exited, please dry your body immediately as no to create a pool of water on the floor creating a slipping hazard. 7. Tips on the Ice Bath: As someone enters the ice bath, it can cause the body to go in a state of shock, Synetic nervous system (fight or flight response). Techniques like box breathing (breath in 4 seconds, hold 4 seconds, breath out 4 seconds, hold 4 seconds). This helps to stimulate your parasynaptic nervous system (parasympathetic nervous system works to conserve energy and facilitate recovery by slowing down the heart rate, dilating blood vessels, and stimulating digestive processes). 1. Increases Energy Efficiency By conserving energy during rest, the PNS allows the body to recharge and repair, improving long-term vitality • . 7. Supports Mental Health Regular activation is linked to lower rates of depression, better emotional resilience, and improved mood stability • How to Activate the Parasympathetic Nervous System Deep breathing (especially diaphragmatic or box breathing)• Cold exposure (like ice baths or cold showers)• Meditation and mindfulness• Gentle yoga or tai chi• Humming, chanting, or singing (stimulates the vagus nerve)• Spending time in nature• To maximise ice baths, someone should have the long term goal of spending 12 minutes submerged neck deep at 4 degrees or lower. In saying this, that would be the equivalent to running a marathon so from a health and safety approach someone should slowly build up to that time, depth and temp in training the body. A beginner should look to start with lower body and for short amount of time. Your skin needs to adapt its skin receptors to the cold water, consistency with the ice bath make it easier for your skin and reduce the "shock" factor. ### General Information
Pelican Park General Information: Different depths of submersion can result in different outcomes:2. Waist deep• Bottom of rib cage• Shoulder depth• Back of the head• Timing of baths:3. General rule to maximize Ice Baths is 1 minute per degree but people can have a lot of variations • Aim for a total of 12 minutes per week, this can be broken up into multiple different sessions • Activating Brown Fat4. Cold water immersion activated Brown Fat - located at the top of the spine and benefits below • 1. Thermogenesis (Heat Production)• 2. Calorie Burning• 3. Blood Sugar Regulation• 4. Improved Metabolic Rate• 5. Fat Reduction• 6. Cardiovascular Protection• Activating the Parasympathetic Nervous System5. Benefits of Parasympathetic Nervous System Activation The PNS counteracts the "fight or flight" response of the sympathetic nervous system. • It promotes calmness, emotional regulation, and mental clarity • . Activation slows the heart rate and dilates blood vessels, helping to reduce blood pressure and cardiovascular strain • . The PNS stimulates saliva production, gastric secretions, and intestinal motility, enhancing nutrient absorption and gut health • . 4. Enhances Sleep Quality By promoting relaxation, the PNS supports deeper, more restorative sleep, especially during non-REM stages • . https://open.spotify.com/episode/5VoFdcD6aYzSyB674NpGPD?si=yB3g_i8PS2W7jM8GzgqroA https://open.spotify.com/episode/6q9YmQvC5fBtHGMYFYqvor?si=495fc490825b42f4 https://open.spotify.com/episode/3iWIAFfzzHWuYCVKvA5VJc?si=AyArqEkESKqMxXq-akr2IA COMPRESSION BOOTS Here’s a step-by-step guide on how to use compression boots, including how to put them on, take them off, how long to use them, and their benefits: How to Use Compression Boots ✅1. Setup Find a comfortable spot to sit or recline (e.g., couch, recliner, or massage chair).• Plug in the compression boot system and ensure the control unit is working.• Check the boots for any damage or wear before use.• 2. Putting on the Boots Unzip or open the boots fully.• Slide your legs in, ensuring your feet are snug at the bottom.• Align the boots properly so the compression zones match your calves, knees, and thighs.• Zip or fasten the boots securely but not too tight—comfort is key.• Beginner: Start with 15–20 minutes.• Regular Use: 30–45 minutes per session.• Maximum: Up to 60 minutes, depending on your recovery needs and manufacturer guidelines. • Use 1–2 times per day, especially after intense workouts or long periods of standing.• Use the control unit to: Select compression intensity (low, medium, high).• Choose massage mode (sequential, pulse, wave, etc.).• Set session duration.• • Start with low to medium pressure if you're new, and increase gradually based on comfort. Relax and stay hydrated.• Avoid crossing your legs or moving excessively.• You can read, meditate, or watch TV during the session.• 6. Taking Off the Boots Turn off the machine and unplug it.• Unzip or unfasten the boots gently.• Slide your legs out slowly to avoid dizziness.• Clean the boots with a damp cloth if needed, and store them in a dry place.• Benefits of Compression Boots Recovery & Circulation Boosts blood flow and lymphatic drainage• Helps flush out lactic acid and metabolic waste• Reduces Muscle Soreness Eases DOMS (Delayed Onset Muscle Soreness)• Speeds up post-workout recovery• Improves Leg Health Reduces swelling, inflammation, and fatigue• Supports vein health and may help prevent varicose veins• Mental Relaxation Promotes a sense of calm and recovery• Can be part of a self-care or mindfulness routine• https://open.spotify.com/episode/5dKtjS7NnP4X90iFjSyMdN?si=aa19b2fbac2b4113 https://open.spotify.com/episode/36uy7oN2YTbVtk24Beceh1?si=30bcf3b8b88d403e https://open.spotify.com/episode/6c0SeI329qTyrqdzEhT65J?si=236508c0f5484e22 INFRARED SAUNA -DO NOT USE THE SAUNA WHEN WET –IT WILL DAMAGE THE SAUNA -NO TOWEL –NO SAUNA -INFRARED SAUNAS ARE A DRY SAUNA AND DO NOT GO AS HOT AS STEAM SAUNAS Here’s a complete how-to guide for using an infrared sauna, including preparation, session duration, frequency, and benefits: Infrared Sauna Guide 1. Preparation Before Your Session Hydrate: Drink a glass of water 15–30 minutes before your session.• Shower: Take a quick shower to remove lotions, oils, or sweat.• Dress Lightly: Wear a towel, swimsuit, or go nude if in a private setting.• Bring Essentials: Water bottle• Towel (to sit on and wipe sweat)• Optional: book, music, or meditation app• • Beginners: Start with 20-30 minutes.• Regular Users: Gradually increase to 30–45 minutes.• Max Duration: Avoid going beyond 50 minutes in one session.• Tip: Start at a lower temperature (around 40–50°C / 104–122°F) and increase as you get used to it. Tip: Start at a lower temperature (around 40–50°C / 104–122°F) and increase as you get used to it. 3. Frequency of Use Beginners: 2–3 times per week.• Regular Users: 3–5 times per week.• Advanced: Daily use is safe for most people, but always listen to your body.• 4. Benefits of Infrared Sauna Detoxification Promotes sweating to help eliminate toxins like heavy metals and chemicals.• Stress Relief Activates the parasympathetic nervous system, promoting relaxation and mental clarity.• Muscle Recovery Increases blood flow and reduces inflammation, aiding in post-workout recovery.• Mimics moderate exercise by increasing heart rate and circulation.• Better Sleep Helps regulate cortisol and promotes deeper, more restful sleep.• Skin Health Opens pores and improves circulation, which can enhance skin tone and clarity.• Infrared (IR) light is a type of electromagnetic radiation that’s invisible to the human eye but felt as heat. It’s divided into three categories based on wavelength: Types of Infrared Rays Near Infrared (NIR) Wavelength: 0.7 to 1.5 microns• Penetration: Deepest into the skin and tissues• Uses: Boosts cellular energy (ATP production)• Enhances circulation• Supports wound healing and muscle recovery• • Common in: Red light therapy devices• Mid Infrared (MIR) Wavelength: 1.5 to 5.6 microns• Penetration: Moderate depth• Uses: Targets soft tissue• Helps reduce inflammation• Supports pain relief• • Common in: Infrared saunas and therapeutic devices• Far Infrared (FIR) Wavelength: 5.6 to 1000 microns• Penetration: Shallowest, mostly absorbed by the skin• Uses:• Wavelength: 5.6 to 1000 microns• Penetration: Shallowest, mostly absorbed by the skin• Uses: Promotes sweating and detoxification• Improves skin health• Supports relaxation and cardiovascular health• • Common in: Infrared saunas, heating pads, FIR blankets• Quick Comparison Type Wavelength Penetration Key Benefits Common Uses NIR 0.7–1.5 µm Deepest Cellular repair, circulation Red light therapy MIR 1.5–5.6 µm Moderate Pain relief, inflammation Saunas, therapy FIR 5.6–1000 µm Shallow Detox, relaxation Saunas, pads https://open.spotify.com/episode/2aXvkMkx6od2SjDRGCS5Xo?si=07e3313bb8c04222 https://open.spotify.com/episode/29ERcTWJqGsOn94qY375ZZ?si=2fc88de4ff7e45d0 https://open.spotify.com/episode/53Tv4OobfLZrxAHYP3SSAw?si=vyK0vzO-Qmave2AgD4gvQQ Offering 5 day trials even though homepage comes up as 1 day.
