### Membership Prices and Options
Singleton Membership: $60 Joining Fee FA $20 Joining Fee Aquatic Teen Gym Family memberships: 2 Adults and 2 children under 16 (eligible memberships include LTS, Teen Gym & Concession) $57.50/pw Hi Claire, all Family Membership types are now set up in AW. When signing up a family, the children must be enrolled in Learn to Swim in order for the family to qualify for the membership type. Please enrol the children in their classes, then allocate the membership type to the parents that matches the number of family members. For example FAMILY (4) is the membership type for families with 2 children in LTS and 2 adults wanting Full Access Memberships. There should only be one joining fee of $60 applied, to only one of the members. This should help moving forward as there is no requirement to apply ADHOC discounts anymore. Please see the new prices below for more information. Membership Type Weekly Installment Weekly Total (incl. 2x LTS Enrolments) Adult Full Access Family of 4 $10.50 $57.50 As long as the total adds up to the $57.50/wk the arrangement can be 2A on Full Access and 2C in GOswim or 1A on Full Acess and 1C (of the right age) on Full Access Concession + 2C in GOswim/Teen Gym. Whatever the configuration, as long as everyone is the right age for the appropriate membership type and it adds up to the total price. Creche memberships are now $27/week for 1st child and $5/week for any additional children. Timetable 16-june-2025-timetable.pdf SPIN – Group indoor cycling workout where you control the intensity. It’s fun, low impact and burns loads of calories. - Bookings are essential. Les Mills Pump – Features 10 tracks with each focusing on a different muscle group, using barbells, weight plates and body weight. Les Mills Pilates – This class is based around slow controlled movements, with a focus on breath and mobility. Full Body Workout – 30 minute indoor or outdoor high calorie burning class. A mix of interval and strength training. Boxing – A cardiovascular class based on the training used for boxing. It can be done with a partner using pads and gloves or solo using dumbells. Strength – This class uses weight plates and a bar. The focus is to build muscle and learn correct form. Aqua – A low impact but high intensity water aerobics class designed to improve flexibility, range of motion, strength and cardiovascular endurance. Yoga – Yoga focuses on the alignment of the whole body, holding poses that support the spine and bring awareness of breath with movement. Stretch – A gentle stretch class for all levels of flexibility. FAMFIT– A family-based fitness class, where children off all ages are welcome, where the kids can get involved or do their own thing while the adults get in a killer strength or cardio workout. Circuit– High energy and fast-paced, move your way around different exercise stations, performing each exercise as many times as possible in a set time. Gold Classes– Best-suited for over 55s age group but open to everyone! Grit/Pilates Combo – 30 minutes HIIT workout followed by 30 minutes of improving flexibility and strength through controlled movements. HIIT – High Intensity Interval Training with minimal rest periods. DanceFit Aqua – Everything Zumba with water resistance , with less impact on joints. Teen Gym – Specially designed group fitness class for teens aged 11-15 years, providing an introduction to the gym floor and fitness. Adult Fit Squad – Want to improve on your swimming, strokes, fitness and possibly improve for your next triathlon? This class is for you, suited to all swimming levels. 16 JUNE 2025 TIM... You can choose from end of term activities through to programs that are energised, alternative and or educational. We offer school swimming program options that are available and aligned with education requirements for water safety. The Curriculum We offer a wide range of programs for your group or school to be a part of. The curriculum provides a comprehensive educational framework that enhances knowledge, skill and understanding of safer aquatic participation. The curriculum ensures alignment with and support of learning outcomes and drowning prevention strategies include: The Federal Government's Curriculum Framework Guide. Where the focus is on experiential rather than command teaching. • The World Health Organisation (WHO) Drowning Prevention Implementation Guide a central documented that is acknowledged worldwide. • The Australian Water Safety Council's Water Safety Plan.• AUSTSWIM Learning Pillars Framework is a guiding document for program development, lessons planning and teaching. • School Carnivals and Water Education Are you planning your schools next annual swimming carnival, swimming trials or aquatic fun day? TRAC has got you covered to ensure everyone enjoys a fun and educational school carnival. We have the following facilities available for your use: 25 metre indoor pool• Dedicated change and toilet facilities• Leisure pool• Dedicated schools entrance• Please keep in mind: We want to avoid interruption to facility members as much as possible. General guidelines are in place to reduce the impact of major events on other users of TRAC to ensure members, the general public and event hosts can enjoy all facilites together. Session Times The aquatics coordinator will work with you to discuss, plan and implement suitable programs to meet your school needs. Ensuring everyone has fun in a safe and friendly environment. Program times may vary depending on the duration, number of students, financial considerations and educational needs. ### Group Fitness
TRAC Group Fitness: Group Fitness Thursday, December 01, 2022 12:48 PM Active World FAQ's and step by step instructions Did you know that you can view your class schedule via the app? Open Active world app1. On the home screen, select “My Schedule” 2. In My Schedule, select the child’s schedule that you want to view3. In this screen, you will be able to see the child’s level, the child’s lesson time, where the class is held (which lane) and who the instructor is. 4. To exit and view a different child, select the back arrow. 5. Did you know you can change your bank details? Open the active world app1. On the home page, tap on the menu screen (3 horizontal lines in the top left-hand side) 2. Scroll down to ‘Billing Details’3. Enter new bank or credit card details and save!4. How to view your child’s progression? Open Active World1. Tap the side bar menu (top left-hand corner of the app).2. Under “Pathways” tap on “Member Progress”.3. Select the member (student) that you want to view and program (GOswim) and then press “Show Pathway”. 4. The GOswim pathway of your child will then show up. 5. Selecting the most recent highlighted character will allow you to view the student’s individual skills in their current level. They will have the following progressions under each skill Working on iti. Nearly thereii. Completediii. a. 6. Tap on the member's name up the top of the page to view a different student on your account.7. Did you know you can change your child’s class via the Active World app? Open Active World1. On the home page go to “Manage My Account” 2. Select “change class” on the child’s class that you want to change3. All available classes for the level that your child in currently in will pop up4. Select the class that is most suitable for you and then select ‘book’. This will change your child’s permanent booking. Active World will let you know that date of the new class Please note, that you cannot move up a level on Active World. If you have received notice that your child is ready to move up, please see our friendly GOswim staff to make that change for you. a. DO NOT “book weekly lesson” to change classes. This creates an entirely new booking for your child with an additional charge. b. 5. Active World Mobile App FAQ Thursday, April 11, 2024 3:49 PM

### GOswim Learn to Swim
Te Hiku GOswim Learn to Swim: The Swim Tangaroa program is designed to encourage and assist whānau (families) to develop Swimming and Water Safety skills through participating in a variety of fun and safe activities in the water. The Swim Tangaroa program makes swimming and water safety a fun experience and helps students learn both in and out of the pool. Catering To All Skill Levels - the graded levels in Swim Tangaroa ensure that everyone can take part no matter what their skill level or experience is. • Suitable For All Ages - Swim Tangaroa lessons are designed to cater for all ages from as young as 6 months up to teenagers and adults. • Access & Inclusion - Swim Tangaroa lessons are easily modified and adapted to suit any specific needs, whether you need one on one lessons or extra time – your specific needs can be met. • Prices for the Swim Tangaroa learn to swim lessons are: Infants (6m – 3yrs) $8.90 per lesson ($89.00 upfront) Pre School (3yrs – 5yrs) $12.90 per lesson ($129.00 upfront) School Age & Squads $12.90 per lesson ($159.00 upfront) Squads swimming x 2 per week 20% off second set of lessons Adults $15.90 per lesson ($159.00 upfront) All upfront fees must be paid prior to the term commencing. Fees can be paid at the pool reception. Swimming Curriculum The curriculum covers five areas of learning. These areas are combined and presented as activities to enhance the students’ learning and development. Key learning areas include: Safe entries and exits• Balance, movement, and recovery• Breath control, submersion, and readiness• Water safety• Swimming stroke development• Swim School –Commencing Term 3 (22nd July) Thursday, December 01, 2022 12:31 PM

All members will be emailed using their contact details saved in Active World on 4 November 2025. What is happening? In December, the WaterMarc health club is getting a fresh new look and a full brand-new suite of TechnoGym equipment. While the gym is being renovated and the equipment installed, it will be closed with no access to 24/7. There will be a pop-up gym and reciprocal rights access to other facilities in Banyule. When is it happening? Works commence in December. All of Level 1 will close for ONE DAY ONLY on December 1. From December 2, Full Access and Premium members will be able to use the pop-up gyms, the cycle studio and the functional training room** **outside of class times and will be subject to closure for some works What is happening with my membership? All memberships will remain active while the gym upgrade takes place. There are many options to continue with your exercise routine including, pop-up gym spaces, reciprocal access at Macleod & Ivanhoe as well as group fitness and aquatic facilities. What about the 1-day closure? All memberships will receive a credit for the 1-day closure on 1 December. This will be applied automatically; you don’t need to do anything. When will the gym re-open? The gym will remain closed from December 1 –December 19. The gym will re-open to members on December 20. Can I still access 24/7? No, due to the temporary nature of the pop-up, 24/7 access will be disabled. This access will be reactivated when the gym opens on December 20. How do I access other Banyule facilities? All WaterMarc members will need to present their membership band at either Macleod Recreation or Ivanhoe Aquatic. Both facilities will require you to check-in with you contact and membership details. Where will there be a pop-up gym? Equipment will be distributed across the Wellbeing studio and Childcare room. Members will also have access to the Functional Training room outside of class times. The Functional Training room will be closed at some stages for painting works and equipment install. Will the pop-up gym be staffed? Health club upgrade Tuesday, November 04, 2025 5:24 PM There will be gym instructors rostered as usual throughout the pop-up gym spaces. We will continue delivering appointments during this period also. Can I do personal training sessions? Yes. Access will be available for all our usual services. However, please check with your trainer to confirm their availability over this period. Will there be Wellness classes running? Yes! The group fitness timetable has had some location changes to ensure impact is minimised. The timetable will be published soon with minimal changes to class availability. Will I be able to use childcare during this period? Our members who currently use the childcare space will receive a separate email with more information regarding this service. While the gym is closed, this space will be repurposed to house a temporary gym. For any members who need this service, we are offering access to Mill Park. How do I access childcare services at Mill Park? All interested members who have made a childcare booking in the last 6 months will need to complete an expression of interest form to register for Mill Park access. Members can complete a registration of interest via the link in their email or using the QR code in the Childcare foyer. What can I access at Mill Park? Members will be able to utilize Health Club, Aquatic Areas and Group Fitness with an active WaterMarc membership when they have a childcare booking. What days can I book Mill Park? Mill Park operates their childcare service on Monday, Tuesday & Thursday every week. Rosa and Michele will be working there on these days, so all children will have a familiar face.

### Membership Prices and Options
WaterMarc Membership: What is Reformer Pilates? Reformer Pilates is a full-body workout designed to enhance strength, coordination, and mobility using a machine with adjustable springs for resistance. The workout focuses on slow, controlled movements with an emphasis on core activation and proper alignment. Classes incorporate a mix of static and dynamic exercises, which can vary from low intensity to more athletic movements. A key advantage of Reformer Pilates is its low-impact nature, making it gentle on the joints while still providing an effective and challenging workout. The adjustable resistance helps tone muscles, improve posture, increase flexibility, and build core strength. Please note that Reformer Pilates may not be suitable for individuals who are injured or recovering from an injury, unless prior approval has been given by an instructor or medical professional. Whether your goal is to increase strength, recover under professional guidance, or improve overall fitness, Reformer Pilates offers a versatile and effective solution. We do not offer trials for reformer Pilates classes and there’s no concession rate. There will be 13 reformer beds. Does Fitness Passport include Reformer Pilates?• > Fitness passport members will not have access to Reformer Pilates classes as it's a premium WaterMarc membership. They have 2 options for this: pay casually $43.90 a class or purchase/upgrade to a premium membership with WaterMarc for $43.90 per week. Will these reformer pilates classes be pregnancy safe?• > We have a pre and postnatal class that runs once per week which they can join. Just like all group fitness classes, the pregnant lady should consult with their GP if it’s safe to do it. Everyone is different. Is there an option to trial a couple of classes before committing to the premium membership to see if it’s worth cancelling my existing pilates membership? • Reformer Pilates Wednesday, April 09, 2025 10:59 AM membership to see if it’s worth cancelling my existing pilates membership? Is/will there be a seniors rate for this membership?• > We do not offer trials for reformer Pilates classes. > There is no concession or seniors rate. How many reformer beds will there be?• How many classes per week planned for reformer pilates? • How many members in each class/instructor to members ratio?• Any classes planned on weekends?• > There will be 13 reformer beds. > There will be one instructor who will not be using one of the 13 beds. > We've started off with 33 classes per week; some class times will be more popular than others but we'll see how everything goes when we launch. ### Pool Facilities
Whitlam Leisure Centre Pool Facilities: Whitlam features five aquatic pools. Outdoor 50m heated swimming pool. Indoor 25m heated pool. Outdoor heated family fun pool with ramp access. Indoor heated toddler pool. Indoor heated wading pool. Indoor spa temperature 36-37 degrees and dry sauna temperature 70-80 degrees. Outdoor pools operate seasonally closed from 7th April to 5th October 2025. Supervision policy Actively supervise children in water under 5 years within arms reach at all times. Parents must remain on site when children under 16 are at facility. Pool temperatures maintained for comfort and safety. Appropriate swimwear must be worn at all times. Outdoor pool closes one hour before indoor pools.

Whitlam Leisure Centre Gym and Fitness Facilities: Health Club spans 1600 square metres featuring state-of-the-art cardiovascular equipment comprehensive weight training area with lifting rigs and bumper plates. Two brand new group exercise studios available. Wellness Studio for yoga and pilates classes. HIIT Zone with qualified Personal Trainer-led classes. Over 40 weekly group fitness classes including LesMills programs GRIT SHAPES BODYCOMBAT CORE BODYATTACK BODYPUMP BODYBALANCE. Gold Active program for seniors 50 plus with discounted membership and free exercise guidance. Personal trainers specialize in general fitness weight loss wellness functional training bodybuilding rehabilitation services.

Our PGA-qualified golf professional Brock Gillard has a variety of repair services available: Re-shafts: steel or graphite, or woods and irons• Length: cut down and extension of clubs• Lie/Loft: Brock uses a lie/loft machine to adjust lie angle and loft• Regrip: Large selection of grips with a variety of different widths to suit every hand size available • Fitting Upgrade your performance with a new set of fitted Golf Clubs! Our PGA qualified golf Professional Brock Gillard has the expert knowledge to fit you with the right set of clubs for your game. Bookings available Monday to Sunday – only from 2pm onwards Future Golf Members Wednesday, February 05, 2025 12:21 PM We want you to feel comfortable while you are playing golf, exercising, or having a drink at the bar. That's why we are pretty relaxed here at Yarrambat Park Golf Course. However, we do have standards because health, safety, and the comfort of our guests is important to us.
